# Image credits

Photos are sourced from [Wikimedia Commons](https://commons.wikimedia.org/)
(species article lead images) and [iNaturalist](https://www.inaturalist.org/)
(taxon and research-grade observation photos). Every photo's license permits
commercial reuse (public domain, CC0, CC BY, or CC BY-SA); the app shows the
artist and license wherever a photo is displayed. Cultivars and trade forms
of one species share the base species' photo. Four fish ship separately
hand-picked bundled images and are not listed here.
